	    [37m# Make sure the xrpath contains only unique directories.[39;49;00m$
	    [34mcase[39;49;00m [33m"[39;49;00m[31m$xrpath[39;49;00m[33m [39;49;00m[33m"[39;49;00m [34min[39;49;00m$
	    *[33m"[39;49;00m[33m [39;49;00m[31m$dir[39;49;00m[33m [39;49;00m[33m"[39;49;00m*) ;;$
	    *) [31mxrpath[39;49;00m=[33m"[39;49;00m[31m$xrpath[39;49;00m[33m [39;49;00m[31m$dir[39;49;00m[33m"[39;49;00m ;;$
	    [34mesac[39;49;00m$
	  [34mfi[39;49;00m$
	  [31mdeplibs[39;49;00m=[33m"[39;49;00m[31m$deplib[39;49;00m[33m [39;49;00m[31m$deplibs[39;49;00m[33m"[39;49;00m$
	  [34mcontinue[39;49;00m$
	  ;;$
	*.la) [31mlib[39;49;00m=[33m"[39;49;00m[31m$deplib[39;49;00m[33m"[39;49;00m ;;$
	*.[31m$libext[39;49;00m)$
	  [34mif[39;49;00m [36mtest[39;49;00m [33m"[39;49;00m[31m$pass[39;49;00m[33m"[39;49;00m = conv; [34mthen[39;49;00m$
	    [31mdeplibs[39;49;00m=[33m"[39;49;00m[31m$deplib[39;49;00m[33m [39;49;00m[31m$deplibs[39;49;00m[33m"[39;49;00m$
	    [34mcontinue[39;49;00m$
	  [34mfi[39;49;00m$
	  [34mcase[39;49;00m [31m$linkmode[39;49;00m [34min[39;49;00m$
	  lib)$
	    [31mvalid_a_lib[39;49;00m=no$
	    [34mcase[39;49;00m [31m$deplibs_check_method[39;49;00m [34min[39;49;00m$
	      match_pattern*)$
		[36mset[39;49;00m dummy [31m$deplibs_check_method[39;49;00m$
	        [31mmatch_pattern_regex[39;49;00m=[33m`[39;49;00mexpr [33m"[39;49;00m[31m$deplibs_check_method[39;49;00m[33m"[39;49;00m : [33m"[39;49;00m[31m$2[39;49;00m[33m \(.*\)[39;49;00m[33m"[39;49;00m[33m`[39;49;00m$
		[34mif[39;49;00m [36meval[39;49;00m [31m$echo[39;49;00m [33m\"[39;49;00m[31m$deplib[39;49;00m[33m\"[39;49;00m [34m2[39;49;00m>/dev/null [33m\[39;49;00m$
		    | [31m$SED[39;49;00m 10q [33m\[39;49;00m$
		    | [31m$EGREP[39;49;00m [33m"[39;49;00m[31m$match_pattern_regex[39;49;00m[33m"[39;49;00m > /dev/null; [34mthen[39;49;00m$
		  [31mvalid_a_lib[39;49;00m=yes$
		[34mfi[39;49;00m$
		;;$
	      pass_all)$
		[31mvalid_a_lib[39;49;00m=yes$
		;;$
            [34mesac[39;49;00m$
	    [34mif[39;49;00m [36mtest[39;49;00m [33m"[39;49;00m[31m$valid_a_lib[39;49;00m[33m"[39;49;00m != yes; [34mthen[39;49;00m$
	      [31m$echo[39;49;00m$
	      [31m$echo[39;49;00m [33m"[39;49;00m[33m*** Warning: Trying to link with static lib archive [39;49;00m[31m$deplib[39;49;00m[33m.[39;49;00m[33m"[39;49;00m$
	      [31m$echo[39;49;00m [33m"*** I have the capability to make that library automatically link in when"[39;49;00m$
	      [31m$echo[39;49;00m [33m"*** you link to this library.  But I can only do this if you have a"[39;49;00m$
	      [31m$echo[39;49;00m [33m"*** shared version of the library, which you do not appear to have"[39;49;00m$
	      [31m$echo[39;49;00m [33m"[39;49;00m[33m*** because the file extensions .[39;49;00m[31m$libext[39;49;00m[33m of this argument makes me believe[39;49;00m[33m"[39;49;00m$
	      [31m$echo[39;49;00m [33m"*** that it is just a static archive that I should not used here."[39;49;00m$
	    [34melse[39;49;00m$
	      [31m$echo[39;49;00m$
	      [31m$echo[39;49;00m [33m"[39;49;00m[33m*** Warning: Linking the shared library [39;49;00m[31m$output[39;49;00m[33m against the[39;49;00m[33m"[39;49;00m$
	      [31m$echo[39;49;00m [33m"[39;49;00m[33m*** static library [39;49;00m[31m$deplib[39;49;00m[33m is not portable![39;49;00m[33m"[39;49;00m$
	      [31mdeplibs[39;49;00m=[33m"[39;49;00m[31m$deplib[39;49;00m[33m [39;49;00m[31m$deplibs[39;49;00m[33m"[39;49;00m$
	    [34mfi[39;49;00m$
	    [34mcontinue[39;49;00m$
	    ;;$
	  prog)$
	    [34mif[39;49;00m [36mtest[39;49;00m [33m"[39;49;00m[31m$pass[39;49;00m[33m"[39;49;00m != link; [34mthen[39;49;00m$
	      [31mdeplibs[39;49;00m=[33m"[39;49;00m[31m$deplib[39;49;00m[33m [39;49;00m[31m$deplibs[39;49;00m[33m"[39;49;00m$
	    [34melse[39;49;00m$
	      [31mcompile_deplibs[39;49;00m=[33m"[39;49;00m[31m$deplib[39;49;00m[33m [39;49;00m[31m$compile_deplibs[39;49;00m[33m"[39;49;00m$
	      [31mfinalize_deplibs[39;49;00m=[33m"[39;49;00m[31m$deplib[39;49;00m[33m [39;49;00m[31m$finalize_deplibs[39;49;00m[33m"[39;49;00m$
	    [34mfi[39;49;00m$
	    [34mcontinue[39;49;00m$
	    ;;$
	  [34mesac[39;49;00m [37m# linkmode[39;49;00m$
	  ;; [37m# *.$libext[39;49;00m$
	*.lo | *.[31m$objext[39;49;00m)$
	  [34mif[39;49;00m [36mtest[39;49;00m [33m"[39;49;00m[31m$pass[39;49;00m[33m"[39;49;00m = conv; [34mthen[39;49;00m$
	    [31mdeplibs[39;49;00m=[33m"[39;49;00m[31m$deplib[39;49;00m[33m [39;49;00m[31m$deplibs[39;49;00m[33m"[39;49;00m$
	  [34melif[39;49;00m [36mtest[39;49;00m [33m"[39;49;00m[31m$linkmode[39;49;00m[33m"[39;49;00m = prog; [34mthen[39;49;00m$
	    [34mif[39;49;00m [36mtest[39;49;00m [33m"[39;49;00m[31m$pass[39;49;00m[33m"[39;49;00m = dlpreopen || [36mtest[39;49;00m [33m"[39;49;00m[31m$dlopen_support[39;49;00m[33m"[39;49;00m != yes || [36mtest[39;49;00m [33m"[39;49;00m[31m$build_libtool_libs[39;49;00m[33m"[39;49;00m = no; [34mthen[39;49;00m$
	      [37m# If there is no dlopen support or we're linking statically,[39;49;00m$
	      [37m# we need to preload.[39;49;00m$
	      [31mnewdlprefiles[39;49;00m=[33m"[39;49;00m[31m$newdlprefiles[39;49;00m[33m [39;49;00m[31m$deplib[39;49;00m[33m"[39;49;00m$
	      [31mcompile_deplibs[39;49;00m=[33m"[39;49;00m[31m$deplib[39;49;00m[33m [39;49;00m[31m$compile_deplibs[39;49;00m[33m"[39;49;00m$
	      [31mfinalize_deplibs[39;49;00m=[33m"[39;49;00m[31m$deplib[39;49;00m[33m [39;49;00m[31m$finalize_deplibs[39;49;00m[33m"[39;49;00m$
	    [34melse[39;49;00m$
	      [31mnewdlfiles[39;49;00m=[33m"[39;49;00m[31m$newdlfiles[39;49;00m[33m [39;49;00m[31m$deplib[39;49;00m[33m"[39;49;00m$
	    [34mfi[39;49;00m$
	  [34mfi[39;49;00m$
	  [34mcontinue[39;49;00m$
	  ;;$
	%DEPLIBS%)$
	  [31malldeplibs[39;49;00m=yes$
	  [34mcontinue[39;49;00m$
	  ;;$
	[34mesac[39;49;00m [37m# case $deplib[39;49;00m$
	[34mif[39;49;00m [36mtest[39;49;00m [33m"[39;49;00m[31m$found[39;49;00m[33m"[39;49;00m = yes || [36mtest[39;49;00m -f [33m"[39;49;00m[31m$lib[39;49;00m[33m"[39;49;00m; [34mthen[39;49;00m :$
	[34melse[39;49;00m$
	  [31m$echo[39;49;00m [33m"[39;49;00m[31m$modename[39;49;00m[33m: cannot find the library \`[39;49;00m[31m$lib[39;49;00m[33m' or unhandled argument \`[39;49;00m[31m$deplib[39;49;00m[33m'[39;49;00m[33m"[39;49;00m [34m1[39;49;00m>&[34m2[39;49;00m$
	  [36mexit[39;49;00m [31m$EXIT_FAILURE[39;49;00m$
	[34mfi[39;49;00m$
$
	[37m# Check to see that this really is a libtool archive.[39;49;00m$
	[34mif[39;49;00m ([33m${[39;49;00m[31mSED[39;49;00m[33m}[39;49;00m -e [33m'2q'[39;49;00m [31m$lib[39;49;00m | grep [33m"[39;49;00m[33m^# Generated by .*[39;49;00m[31m$PACKAGE[39;49;00m[33m"[39;49;00m) >/dev/null [34m2[39;49;00m>&[34m1[39;49;00m; [34mthen[39;49;00m :$
	[34melse[39;49;00m$
	  [31m$echo[39;49;00m [33m"[39;49;00m[31m$modename[39;49;00m[33m: \`[39;49;00m[31m$lib[39;49;00m[33m' is not a valid libtool archive[39;49;00m[33m"[39;49;00m [34m1[39;49;00m>&[34m2[39;49;00m$
	  [36mexit[39;49;00m [31m$EXIT_FAILURE[39;49;00m$
	[34mfi[39;49;00m$
$
	[31mladir[39;49;00m=[33m`[39;49;00m[31m$echo[39;49;00m [33m"[39;49;00m[33mX[39;49;00m[31m$lib[39;49;00m[33m"[39;49;00m | [31m$Xsed[39;49;00m -e [33m's%/[^/]*$%%'[39;49;00m[33m`[39;49;00m$
	[36mtest[39;49;00m [33m"[39;49;00m[33mX[39;49;00m[31m$ladir[39;49;00m[33m"[39;49;00m = [33m"[39;49;00m[33mX[39;49;00m[31m$lib[39;49;00m[33m"[39;49;00m && [31mladir[39;49;00m=[33m"."[39;49;00m$
$
	[31mdlname[39;49;00m=$
	[31mdlopen[39;49;00m=$
	[31mdlpreopen[39;49;00m=$
	[31mlibdir[39;49;00m=$
	[31mlibrary_names[39;49;00m=$
	[31mold_library[39;49;00m=$
	[37m# If the library was installed with an old release of libtool,[39;49;00m$
	[37m# it will not redefine variables installed, or shouldnotlink[39;49;00m$
	[31minstalled[39;49;00m=yes$
	[31mshouldnotlink[39;49;00m=no$
	[31mavoidtemprpath[39;49;00m=$
$
$
	[37m# Read the .la file[39;49;00m$
	[34mcase[39;49;00m [31m$lib[39;49;00m [34min[39;49;00m$
	*/* | *[33m\\[39;49;00m*) . [31m$lib[39;49;00m ;;$
	*) . ./[31m$lib[39;49;00m ;;$
	[34mesac[39;49;00m$
$
	[34mif[39;49;00m [36mtest[39;49;00m [33m"[39;49;00m[31m$linkmode[39;49;00m[33m,[39;49;00m[31m$pass[39;49;00m[33m"[39;49;00m = [33m"lib,link"[39;49;00m ||$
	   [36mtest[39;49;00m [33m"[39;49;00m[31m$linkmode[39;49;00m[33m,[39;49;00m[31m$pass[39;49;00m[33m"[39;49;00m = [33m"prog,scan"[39;49;00m ||$
	   { [36mtest[39;49;00m [33m"[39;49;00m[31m$linkmode[39;49;00m[33m"[39;49;00m != prog && [36mtest[39;49;00m [33m"[39;49;00m[31m$linkmode[39;49;00m[33m"[39;49;00m != lib; }; [34mthen[39;49;00m$
	  [36mtest[39;49;00m -n [33m"[39;49;00m[31m$dlopen[39;49;00m[33m"[39;49;00m && [31mdlfiles[39;49;00m=[33m"[39;49;00m[31m$dlfiles[39;49;00m[33m [39;49;00m[31m$dlopen[39;49;00m[33m"[39;49;00m$
	  [36mtest[39;49;00m -n [33m"[39;49;00m[31m$dlpreopen[39;49;00m[33m"[39;49;00m && [31mdlprefiles[39;49;00m=[33m"[39;49;00m[31m$dlprefiles[39;49;00m[33m [39;49;00m[31m$dlpreopen[39;49;00m[33m"[39;49;00m$
	[34mfi[39;49;00m$
$
	[34mif[39;49;00m [36mtest[39;49;00m [33m"[39;49;00m[31m$pass[39;49;00m[33m"[39;49;00m = conv; [34mthen[39;49;00m$
	  [37m# Only check for convenience libraries[39;49;00m$
	  [31mdeplibs[39;49;00m=[33m"[39;49;00m[31m$lib[39;49;00m[33m [39;49;00m[31m$deplibs[39;49;00m[33m"[39;49;00m$
	  [34mif[39;49;00m [36mtest[39;49;00m -z [33m"[39;49;00m[31m$libdir[39;49;00m[33m"[39;49;00m; [34mthen[39;49;00m$
	    [34mif[39;49;00m [36mtest[39;49;00m -z [33m"[39;49;00m[31m$old_library[39;49;00m[33m"[39;49;00m; [34mthen[39;49;00m$
	      [31m$echo[39;49;00m [33m"[39;49;00m[31m$modename[39;49;00m[33m: cannot find name of link library for \`[39;49;00m[31m$lib[39;49;00m[33m'[39;49;00m[33m"[39;49;00m [34m1[39;49;00m>&[34m2[39;49;00m$
	      [36mexit[39;49;00m [31m$EXIT_FAILURE[39;49;00m$
	    [34mfi[39;49;00m$
	    [37m# It is a libtool convenience library, so add in its objects.[39;49;00m$
	    [31mconvenience[39;49;00m=[33m"[39;49;00m[31m$convenience[39;49;00m[33m [39;49;00m[31m$ladir[39;49;00m[33m/[39;49;00m[31m$objdir[39;49;00m[33m/[39;49;00m[31m$old_library[39;49;00m[33m"[39;49;00m$
	    [31mold_convenience[39;49;00m=[33m"[39;49;00m[31m$old_convenience[39;49;00m[33m [39;49;00m[31m$ladir[39;49;00m[33m/[39;49;00m[31m$objdir[39;49;00m[33m/[39;49;00m[31m$old_library[39;49;00m[33m"[39;49;00m$
	    [31mtmp_libs[39;49;00m=$
	    [34mfor[39;49;00m deplib [34min[39;49;00m [31m$dependency_libs[39;49;00m; [34mdo[39;49;00m$
	      [31mdeplibs[39;49;00m=[33m"[39;49;00m[31m$deplib[39;49;00m[33m [39;49;00m[31m$deplibs[39;49;00m[33m"[39;49;00m$
              [34mif[39;49;00m [36mtest[39;49;00m [33m"[39;49;00m[33mX[39;49;00m[31m$duplicate_deps[39;49;00m[33m"[39;49;00m = [33m"Xyes"[39;49;00m ; [34mthen[39;49;00m$
	        [34mcase[39;49;00m [33m"[39;49;00m[31m$tmp_libs[39;49;00m[33m [39;49;00m[33m"[39;49;00m [34min[39;49;00m$
	        *[33m"[39;49;00m[33m [39;49;00m[31m$deplib[39;49;00m[33m [39;49;00m[33m"[39;49;00m*) [31mspecialdeplibs[39;49;00m=[33m"[39;49;00m[31m$specialdeplibs[39;49;00m[33m [39;49;00m[31m$deplib[39;49;00m[33m"[39;49;00m ;;$
	        [34mesac[39;49;00m$
              [34mfi[39;49;00m$
	      [31mtmp_libs[39;49;00m=[33m"[39;49;00m[31m$tmp_libs[39;49;00m[33m [39;49;00m[31m$deplib[39;49;00m[33m"[39;49;00m$
	    [34mdone[39;49;00m$
	  [34melif[39;49;00m [36mtest[39;49;00m [33m"[39;49;00m[31m$linkmode[39;49;00m[33m"[39;49;00m != prog && [36mtest[39;49;00m [33m"[39;49;00m[31m$linkmode[39;49;00m[33m"[39;49;00m != lib; [34mthen[39;49;00m$
	    [31m$echo[39;49;00m [33m"[39;49;00m[31m$modename[39;49;00m[33m: \`[39;49;00m[31m$lib[39;49;00m[33m' is not a convenience library[39;49;00m[33m"[39;49;00m [34m1[39;49;00m>&[34m2[39;49;00m$
	    [36mexit[39;49;00m [31m$EXIT_FAILURE[39;49;00m$
	  [34mfi[39;49;00m$
	  [34mcontinue[39;49;00m$
	[34mfi[39;49;00m [37m# $pass = conv[39;49;00m$
$
$
	[37m# Get the name of the library we link against.[39;49;00m$
	[31mlinklib[39;49;00m=$
	[34mfor[39;49;00m l [34min[39;49;00m [31m$old_library[39;49;00m [31m$library_names[39;49;00m; [34mdo[39;49;00m$
	  [31mlinklib[39;49;00m=[33m"[39;49;00m[31m$l[39;49;00m[33m"[39;49;00m$
	[34mdone[39;49;00m$
	[34mif[39;49;00m [36mtest[39;49;00m -z [33m"[39;49;00m[31m$linklib[39;49;00m[33m"[39;49;00m; [34mthen[39;49;00m$
	  [31m$echo[39;49;00m [33m"[39;49;00m[31m$modename[39;49;00m[33m: cannot find name of link library for \`[39;49;00m[31m$lib[39;49;00m[33m'[39;49;00m[33m"[39;49;00m [34m1[39;49;00m>&[34m2[39;49;00m$
	  [36mexit[39;49;00m [31m$EXIT_FAILURE[39;49;00m$
	[34mfi[39;49;00m$
$
	[37m# This library was specified with -dlopen.[39;49;00m$
	[34mif[39;49;00m [36mtest[39;49;00m [33m"[39;49;00m[31m$pass[39;49;00m[33m"[39;49;00m = dlopen; [34mthen[39;49;00m$
	  [34mif[39;49;00m [36mtest[39;49;00m -z [33m"[39;49;00m[31m$libdir[39;49;00m[33m"[39;49;00m; [34mthen[39;49;00m$
	    [31m$echo[39;49;00m [33m"[39;49;00m[31m$modename[39;49;00m[33m: cannot -dlopen a convenience library: \`[39;49;00m[31m$lib[39;49;00m[33m'[39;49;00m[33m"[39;49;00m [34m1[39;49;00m>&[34m2[39;49;00m$
	    [36mexit[39;49;00m [31m$EXIT_FAILURE[39;49;00m$
	  [34mfi[39;49;00m$
	  [34mif[39;49;00m [36mtest[39;49;00m -z [33m"[39;49;00m[31m$dlname[39;49;00m[33m"[39;49;00m ||$
	     [36mtest[39;49;00m [33m"[39;49;00m[31m$dlopen_support[39;49;00m[33m"[39;49;00m != yes ||$
	     [36mtest[39;49;00m [33m"[39;49;00m[31m$build_libtool_libs[39;49;00m[33m"[39;49;00m = no; [34mthen[39;49;00m$
	    [37m# If there is no dlname, no dlopen support or we're linking[39;49;00m$
	    [37m# statically, we need to preload.  We also need to preload any[39;49;00m$
	    [37m# dependent libraries so libltdl's deplib preloader doesn't[39;49;00m$
	    [37m# bomb out in the load deplibs phase.[39;49;00m$
	    [31mdlprefiles[39;49;00m=[33m"[39;49;00m[31m$dlprefiles[39;49;00m[33m [39;49;00m[31m$lib[39;49;00m[33m [39;49;00m[31m$dependency_libs[39;49;00m[33m"[39;49;00m$
	  [34melse[39;49;00m$
	    [31mnewdlfiles[39;49;00m=[33m"[39;49;00m[31m$newdlfiles[39;49;00m[33m [39;49;00m[31m$lib[39;49;00m[33m"[39;49;00m$
	  [34mfi[39;49;00m$
	  [34mcontinue[39;49;00m$
	[34mfi[39;49;00m [37m# $pass = dlopen[39;49;00m$
$
	[37m# We need an absolute path.[39;49;00m$
	[34mcase[39;49;00m [31m$ladir[39;49;00m [34min[39;49;00m$
	[[33m\\[39;49;00m/]* | [A-Za-z]:[[33m\\[39;49;00m/]*) [31mabs_ladir[39;49;00m=[33m"[39;49;00m[31m$ladir[39;49;00m[33m"[39;49;00m ;;$
	*)$
	  [31mabs_ladir[39;49;00m=[33m`[39;49;00m[36mcd[39;49;00m [33m"[39;49;00m[31m$ladir[39;49;00m[33m"[39;49;00m && [36mpwd[39;49;00m[33m`[39;49;00m$
	  [34mif[39;49;00m [36mtest[39;49;00m -z [33m"[39;49;00m[31m$abs_ladir[39;49;00m[33m"[39;49;00m; [34mthen[39;49;00m$
	    [31m$echo[39;49;00m [33m"[39;49;00m[31m$modename[39;49;00m[33m: warning: cannot determine absolute directory name of \`[39;49;00m[31m$ladir[39;49;00m[33m'[39;49;00m[33m"[39;49;00m [34m1[39;49;00m>&[34m2[39;49;00m$
	    [31m$echo[39;49;00m [33m"[39;49;00m[31m$modename[39;49;00m[33m: passing it literally to the linker, although it might fail[39;49;00m[33m"[39;49;00m [34m1[39;49;00m>&[34m2[39;49;00m$
	    [31mabs_ladir[39;49;00m=[33m"[39;49;00m[31m$ladir[39;49;00m[33m"[39;49;00m$
	  [34mfi[39;49;00m$
	  ;;$
	[34mesac[39;49;00m$
	[31mlaname[39;49;00m=[33m`[39;49;00m[31m$echo[39;49;00m [33m"[39;49;00m[33mX[39;49;00m[31m$lib[39;49;00m[33m"[39;49;00m | [31m$Xsed[39;49;00m -e [33m's%^.*/%%'[39;49;00m[33m`[39;49;00m$
$
	[37m# Find the relevant object directory and library name.[39;49;00m$
	[34mif[39;49;00m [36mtest[39;49;00m [33m"[39;49;00m[33mX[39;49;00m[31m$installed[39;49;00m[33m"[39;49;00m = Xyes; [34mthen[39;49;00m$
	  [34mif[39;49;00m [36mtest[39;49;00m ! -f [33m"[39;49;00m[31m$libdir[39;49;00m[33m/[39;49;00m[31m$linklib[39;49;00m[33m"[39;49;00m && [36mtest[39;49;00m -f [33m"[39;49;00m[31m$abs_ladir[39;49;00m[33m/[39;49;00m[31m$linklib[39;49;00m[33m"[39;49;00m; [34mthen[39;49;00m$
	    [31m$echo[39;49;00m [33m"[39;49;00m[31m$modename[39;49;00m[33m: warning: library \`[39;49;00m[31m$lib[39;49;00m[33m' was moved.[39;49;00m[33m"[39;49;00m [34m1[39;49;00m>&[34m2[39;49;00m$
	    [31mdir[39;49;00m=[33m"[39;49;00m[31m$ladir[39;49;00m[33m"[39;49;00m$
	    [31mabsdir[39;49;00m=[33m"[39;49;00m[31m$abs_ladir[39;49;00m[33m"[39;49;00m$
	    [31mlibdir[39;49;00m=[33m"[39;49;00m[31m$abs_ladir[39;49;00m[33m"[39;49;00m$
	  [34melse[39;49;00m$
	    [31mdir[39;49;00m=[33m"[39;49;00m[31m$libdir[39;49;00m[33m"[39;49;00m$
	    [31mabsdir[39;49;00m=[33m"[39;49;00m[31m$libdir[39;49;00m[33m"[39;49;00m$
	  [34mfi[39;49;00m$
	  [36mtest[39;49;00m [33m"[39;49;00m[33mX[39;49;00m[31m$hardcode_automatic[39;49;00m[33m"[39;49;00m = Xyes && [31mavoidtemprpath[39;49;00m=yes$
	[34melse[39;49;00m$
	  [34mif[39;49;00m [36mtest[39;49;00m ! -f [33m"[39;49;00m[31m$ladir[39;49;00m[33m/[39;49;00m[31m$objdir[39;49;00m[33m/[39;49;00m[31m$linklib[39;49;00m[33m"[39;49;00m && [36mtest[39;49;00m -f [33m"[39;49;00m[31m$abs_ladir[39;49;00m[33m/[39;49;00m[31m$linklib[39;49;00m[33m"[39;49;00m; [34mthen[39;49;00m$
	    [31mdir[39;49;00m=[33m"[39;49;00m[31m$ladir[39;49;00m[33m"[39;49;00m$
	    [31mabsdir[39;49;00m=[33m"[39;49;00m[31m$abs_ladir[39;49;00m[33m"[39;49;00m$
	    [37m# Remove this search path later[39;49;00m$
	    [31mnotinst_path[39;49;00m=[33m"[39;49;00m[31m$notinst_path[39;49;00m[33m [39;49;00m[31m$abs_ladir[39;49;00m[33m"[39;49;00m$
	  [34melse[39;49;00m$
	    [31mdir[39;49;00m=[33m"[39;49;00m[31m$ladir[39;49;00m[33m/[39;49;00m[31m$objdir[39;49;00m[33m"[39;49;00m$
	    [31mabsdir[39;49;00m=[33m"[39;49;00m[31m$abs_ladir[39;49;00m[33m/[39;49;00m[31m$objdir[39;49;00m[33m"[39;49;00m$
	    [37m# Remove this search path later[39;49;00m$
	    [31mnotinst_path[39;49;00m=[33m"[39;49;00m[31m$notinst_path[39;49;00m[33m [39;49;00m[31m$abs_ladir[39;49;00m[33m"[39;49;00m$
	  [34mfi[39;49;00m$
	[34mfi[39;49;00m [37m# $installed = yes[39;49;00m$
	[31mname[39;49;00m=[33m`[39;49;00m[31m$echo[39;49;00m [33m"[39;49;00m[33mX[39;49;00m[31m$laname[39;49;00m[33m"[39;49;00m | [31m$Xsed[39;49;00m -e [33m's/\.la$//'[39;49;00m -e [33m's/^lib//'[39;49;00m[33m`[39;49;00m$
$
	[37m# This library was specified with -dlpreopen.[39;49;00m$
	[34mif[39;49;00m [36mtest[39;49;00m [33m"[39;49;00m[31m$pass[39;49;00m[33m"[39;49;00m = dlpreopen; [34mthen[39;49;00m$
	  [34mif[39;49;00m [36mtest[39;49;00m -z [33m"[39;49;00m[31m$libdir[39;49;00m[33m"[39;49;00m; [34mthen[39;49;00m$
	    [31m$echo[39;49;00m [33m"[39;49;00m[31m$modename[39;49;00m[33m: cannot -dlpreopen a convenience library: \`[39;49;00m[31m$lib[39;49;00m[33m'[39;49;00m[33m"[39;49;00m [34m1[39;49;00m>&[34m2[39;49;00m$
	    [36mexit[39;49;00m [31m$EXIT_FAILURE[39;49;00m$
	  [34mfi[39;49;00m$
	  [37m# Prefer using a static library (so that no silly _DYNAMIC symbols[39;49;00m$
	  [37m# are required to link).[39;49;00m$
	  [34mif[39;49;00m [36mtest[39;49;00m -n [33m"[39;49;00m[31m$old_library[39;49;00m[33m"[39;49;00m; [34mthen[39;49;00m$
	    [31mnewdlprefiles[39;49;00m=[33m"[39;49;00m[31m$newdlprefiles[39;49;00m[33m [39;49;00m[31m$dir[39;49;00m[33m/[39;49;00m[31m$old_library[39;49;00m[33m"[39;49;00m$
	  [37m# Otherwise, use the dlname, so that lt_dlopen finds it.[39;49;00m$
	  [34melif[39;49;00m [36mtest[39;49;00m -n [33m"[39;49;00m[31m$dlname[39;49;00m[33m"[39;49;00m; [34mthen[39;49;00m$
	    [31mnewdlprefiles[39;49;00m=[33m"[39;49;00m[31m$newdlprefiles[39;49;00m[33m [39;49;00m[31m$dir[39;49;00m[33m/[39;49;00m[31m$dlname[39;49;00m[33m"[39;49;00m$
	  [34melse[39;49;00m$
	    [31mnewdlprefiles[39;49;00m=[33m"[39;49;00m[31m$newdlprefiles[39;49;00m[33m [39;49;00m[31m$dir[39;49;00m[33m/[39;49;00m[31m$linklib[39;49;00m[33m"[39;49;00m$
	  [34mfi[39;49;00m$
	[34mfi[39;49;00m [37m# $pass = dlpreopen[39;49;00m$
$
	[34mif[39;49;00m [36mtest[39;49;00m -z [33m"[39;49;00m[31m$libdir[39;49;00m[33m"[39;49;00m; [34mthen[39;49;00m$
	  [37m# Link the convenience library[39;49;00m$
	  [34mif[39;49;00m [36mtest[39;49;00m [33m"[39;49;00m[31m$linkmode[39;49;00m[33m"[39;49;00m = lib; [34mthen[39;49;00m$
	    [31mdeplibs[39;49;00m=[33m"[39;49;00m[31m$dir[39;49;00m[33m/[39;49;00m[31m$old_library[39;49;00m[33m [39;49;00m[31m$deplibs[39;49;00m[33m"[39;49;00m$
	  [34melif[39;49;00m [36mtest[39;49;00m [33m"[39;49;00m[31m$linkmode[39;49;00m[33m,[39;49;00m[31m$pass[39;49;00m[33m"[39;49;00m = [33m"prog,link"[39;49;00m; [34mthen[39;49;00m$
	    [31mcompile_deplibs[39;49;00m=[33m"[39;49;00m[31m$dir[39;49;00m[33m/[39;49;00m[31m$old_library[39;49;00m[33m [39;49;00m[31m$compile_deplibs[39;49;00m[33m"[39;49;00m$
	    [31mfinalize_deplibs[39;49;00m=[33m"[39;49;00m[31m$dir[39;49;00m[33m/[39;49;00m[31m$old_library[39;49;00m[33m [39;49;00m[31m$finalize_deplibs[39;49;00m[33m"[39;49;00m$
	  [34melse[39;49;00m$
	    [31mdeplibs[39;49;00m=[33m"[39;49;00m[31m$lib[39;49;00m[33m [39;49;00m[31m$deplibs[39;49;00m[33m"[39;49;00m [37m# used for prog,scan pass[39;49;00m$
	  [34mfi[39;49;00m$
	  [34mcontinue[39;49;00m$
	[34mfi[39;49;00m$
$
$
	[34mif[39;49;00m [36mtest[39;49;00m [33m"[39;49;00m[31m$linkmode[39;49;00m[33m"[39;49;00m = prog && [36mtest[39;49;00m [33m"[39;49;00m[31m$pass[39;49;00m[33m"[39;49;00m != link; [34mthen[39;49;00m$
	  [31mnewlib_search_path[39;49;00m=[33m"[39;49;00m[31m$newlib_search_path[39;49;00m[33m [39;49;00m[31m$ladir[39;49;00m[33m"[39;49;00m$
	  [31mdeplibs[39;49;00m=[33m"[39;49;00m[31m$lib[39;49;00m[33m [39;49;00m[31m$deplibs[39;49;00m[33m"[39;49;00m$

	  [31mlinkalldeplibs[39;49;00m=no$
	  [34mif[39;49;00m [36mtest[39;49;00m [33m"[39;49;00m[31m$link_all_deplibs[39;49;00m[33m"[39;49;00m != no || [36mtest[39;49;00m -z [33m"[39;49;00m[31m$library_names[39;49;00m[33m"[39;49;00m ||$
	     [36mtest[39;49;00m [33m"[39;49;00m[31m$build_libtool_libs[39;49;00m[33m"[39;49;00m = no; [34mthen[39;49;00m$
	    [31mlinkalldeplibs[39;49;00m=yes$
	  [34mfi[39;49;00m$

	  [31mtmp_libs[39;49;00m=$
	  [34mfor[39;49;00m deplib [34min[39;49;00m [31m$dependency_libs[39;49;00m; [34mdo[39;49;00m$
	    [34mcase[39;49;00m [31m$deplib[39;49;00m [34min[39;49;00m$
	    -L*) [31mnewlib_search_path[39;49;00m=[33m"[39;49;00m[31m$newlib_search_path[39;49;00m[33m [39;49;00m[33m"[39;49;00m[33m`[39;49;00m[31m$echo[39;49;00m [33m"[39;49;00m[33mX[39;49;00m[31m$deplib[39;49;00m[33m"[39;49;00m | [31m$Xsed[39;49;00m -e [33m's/^-L//'[39;49;00m[33m`[39;49;00m;; [37m### testsuite: skip nested quoting test[39;49;00m$
	    [34mesac[39;49;00m$
	    [37m# Need to link against all dependency_libs?[39;49;00m$
	    [34mif[39;49;00m [36mtest[39;49;00m [33m"[39;49;00m[31m$linkalldeplibs[39;49;00m[33m"[39;49;00m = yes; [34mthen[39;49;00m$

	    [34melse[39;49;00m$
	      [37m# Need to hardcode shared library paths[39;49;00m$
	      [37m# or/and link against static libraries[39;49;00m$

	    [34mfi[39;49;00m$
	    [34mif[39;49;00m [36mtest[39;49;00m [33m"[39;49;00m[33mX[39;49;00m[31m$duplicate_deps[39;49;00m[33m"[39;49;00m = [33m"Xyes"[39;49;00m ; [34mthen[39;49;00m$
	      [34mcase[39;49;00m [33m"[39;49;00m[31m$tmp_libs[39;49;00m[33m [39;49;00m[33m"[39;49;00m [34min[39;49;00m$
	      *[33m"[39;49;00m[33m [39;49;00m[31m$deplib[39;49;00m[33m [39;49;00m[33m"[39;49;00m*) [31mspecialdeplibs[39;49;00m=[33m"[39;49;00m[31m$specialdeplibs[39;49;00m[33m [39;49;00m[31m$deplib[39;49;00m[33m"[39;49;00m ;;$

	    [34mfi[39;49;00m$
	    [31mtmp_libs[39;49;00m=[33m"[39;49;00m[31m$tmp_libs[39;49;00m[33m [39;49;00m[31m$deplib[39;49;00m[33m"[39;49;00m$
	  [34mdone[39;49;00m [37m# for deplib[39;49;00m$
	  [34mcontinue[39;49;00m$
	[34mfi[39;49;00m [37m# $linkmode = prog...[39;49;00m$
$
	[34mif[39;49;00m [36mtest[39;49;00m [33m"[39;49;00m[31m$linkmode[39;49;00m[33m,[39;49;00m[31m$pass[39;49;00m[33m"[39;49;00m = [33m"prog,link"[39;49;00m; [34mthen[39;49;00m$
	  [34mif[39;49;00m [36mtest[39;49;00m -n [33m"[39;49;00m[31m$library_names[39;49;00m[33m"[39;49;00m &&$
	     { [36mtest[39;49;00m [33m"[39;49;00m[31m$prefer_static_libs[39;49;00m[33m"[39;49;00m = no || [36mtest[39;49;00m -z [33m"[39;49;00m[31m$old_library[39;49;00m[33m"[39;49;00m; }; [34mthen[39;49;00m$
	    [37m# We need to hardcode the library path[39;49;00m$
	    [34mif[39;49;00m [36mtest[39;49;00m -n [33m"[39;49;00m[31m$shlibpath_var[39;49;00m[33m"[39;49;00m && [36mtest[39;49;00m -z [33m"[39;49;00m[31m$avoidtemprpath[39;49;00m[33m"[39;49;00m ; [34mthen[39;49;00m$
	      [37m# Make sure the rpath contains only unique directories.[39;49;00m$
	      [34mcase[39;49;00m [33m"[39;49;00m[31m$temp_rpath[39;49;00m[33m [39;49;00m[33m"[39;49;00m [34min[39;49;00m$
	      *[33m"[39;49;00m[33m [39;49;00m[31m$dir[39;49;00m[33m [39;49;00m[33m"[39;49;00m*) ;;$
	      *[33m"[39;49;00m[33m [39;49;00m[31m$absdir[39;49;00m[33m [39;49;00m[33m"[39;49;00m*) ;;$
	      *) [31mtemp_rpath[39;49;00m=[33m"[39;49;00m[31m$temp_rpath[39;49;00m[33m [39;49;00m[31m$absdir[39;49;00m[33m"[39;49;00m ;;$
	      [34mesac[39;49;00m$
	    [34mfi[39;49;00m$
$
	    [37m# Hardcode the library path.[39;49;00m$
	    [37m# Skip directories that are in the system default run-time[39;49;00m$
	    [37m# search path.[39;49;00m$
	    [34mcase[39;49;00m [33m"[39;49;00m[33m [39;49;00m[31m$sys_lib_dlsearch_path[39;49;00m[33m [39;49;00m[33m"[39;49;00m [34min[39;49;00m$
	    *[33m"[39;49;00m[33m [39;49;00m[31m$absdir[39;49;00m[33m [39;49;00m[33m"[39;49;00m*) ;;$
	    *)$
	      [34mcase[39;49;00m [33m"[39;49;00m[31m$compile_rpath[39;49;00m[33m [39;49;00m[33m"[39;49;00m [34min[39;49;00m$
	      *[33m"[39;49;00m[33m [39;49;00m[31m$absdir[39;49;00m[33m [39;49;00m[33m"[39;49;00m*) ;;$
	      *) [31mcompile_rpath[39;49;00m=[33m"[39;49;00m[31m$compile_rpath[39;49;00m[33m [39;49;00m[31m$absdir[39;49;00m[33m"[39;49;00m$
	      [34mesac[39;49;00m$
	      ;;$
	    [34mesac[39;49;00m$
	    [34mcase[39;49;00m [33m"[39;49;00m[33m [39;49;00m[31m$sys_lib_dlsearch_path[39;49;00m[33m [39;49;00m[33m"[39;49;00m [34min[39;49;00m$
	    *[33m"[39;49;00m[33m [39;49;00m[31m$libdir[39;49;00m[33m [39;49;00m[33m"[39;49;00m*) ;;$
